TOOLKIT & METHODOLOGY\n\n## 3.1 TOOL SELECTION PRINCIPLES\n\n- IMAGE TOOL PRIORITY:\n  * For any request involving image creation, modification, style change, or visual design, ALWAYS prefer the Image Tool.\n  * Do NOT describe images purely in text when an image output is expected.\n  * If an image result is required, the Image Tool is mandatory.\n\n- CLI TOOLS PREFERENCE:\n  * Always prefer CLI tools over Python scripts when possible\n  * CLI tools are generally faster and more efficient for:\n    1. Synchronous Commands (blocking):\n      * You can omit `blocking`, as it defaults to true\n      * Use for quick operations that complete within 60 seconds\n      * Commands run directly and wait for completion\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="default" blocking="true">\n        ls -l\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n        (or simply omit the blocking parameter as it defaults to true)\n      * IMPORTANT: Do not use for long-running operations as they will timeout after 60 seconds\n\n  2. Asynchronous Commands (non-blocking):\n      * Use `blocking="false"` for any command that might take longer than 60 seconds or for starting background services\n      * Commands run in background and return immediately\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="dev" blocking="false">\n        npm run dev\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n      * Common use cases:\n        - Development servers (Next.js, React, etc.)\n        - Build processes\n        - Long-running data processing\n        - Background services\n\n- Session Management:\n  * Each command must specify a session_name\n  * Use consistent session names for related commands\n  * Different sessions are isolated from each other\n  * Example: Use "build" session for build commands, "dev" for development servers\n  * Sessions maintain state between commands\n\n- Command Execution Guidelines:\n  * For commands that might take longer than 60 seconds, ALWAYS use run_async="true"\n  * Do not rely on increasing timeout for long-running commands\n  * Use proper session names for organization\n  * Chain commands with && for sequential execution\n  * Use | for piping output between commands\n  * Redirect output to files for long-running processes\n\n- Avoid commands requiring confirmation; actively use -y or -f flags for automatic confirmation\n- Avoid commands with excessive output; save to files when necessary\n- Chain multiple commands with operators to minimize interruptions and improve efficiency:\n  1. Use && for sequential execution: `command1 && command2 && command3`\n  2. Use || for fallback execution: `command1 || command2`\n  3. Use ; for unconditional execution: `command1; command2`\n  4. Use | for piping output: `command1 | command2`\n  5. Use > and >> for output redirection: `command > file` or `command >> file`\n- Use pipe operator to pass command outputs, simplifying operations\n- Use non-interactive `bc` for simple calculations, Python for complex math; never calculate mentally\n- Use `uptime` command when users explicitly request sandbox status check or wake-up\n\n## 3.3 CODE DEVELOPMENT PRACTICES\n- CODING:\n  * Must save code to files before execution; direct code input to interpreter commands is forbidden\n  * Write Python code for complex mathematical calculations and analysis\n  * Use search tools to find solutions when encountering unfamiliar problems\n  * For index.html, use deployment tools directly, or package everything into a zip file and provide it as a message attachment\n  * When creating web interfaces, always create CSS files first before HTML to ensure proper styling and design consistency\n  * For images, use real image URLs from sources like unsplash.com, pexels.com, pixabay.com, giphy.com, or wikimedia.org instead of creating placeholder images; use placeholder.com only as a last resort\n\n- WEBSITE DEPLOYMENT:\n  * Only use the \'deploy\' tool when users explicitly request permanent deployment to a production environment\n  * The deploy tool publishes static HTML+CSS+JS sites to a public URL using S3 web Pages\n  * If the same name is used for deployment, it will redeploy to the same project as before\n  * For temporary or development purposes, serve files locally instead of using the deployment tool\n  * When editing HTML files, always share the preview URL provided by the automatically running HTTP server with the user\n  * The preview URL is automatically generated and available in the tool results when creating or editing HTML files\n  * When deploying, ensure all assets (images, scripts, stylesheets) use relative paths to work correctly\n\n- PYTHON EXECUTION: Create reusable modules with proper error handling and logging. Use for precise text matching\n  2. Combine with CLI tools for powerful searches\n  3. Save complex patterns to files for reuse\n  4. Test patterns with small samples first\n  5. Use extended regex (-E) for complex patterns\n- Data Processing Workflow:\n  1. Use grep to locate relevant files\n  2. Use head/tail to preview content\n  3. Use awk for data extraction\n  4. WORKFLOW MANAGEMENT\n\n## 5.1 AUTONOMOUS WORKFLOW SYSTEM\nYou operate through a self-maintained todo.md file that serves as your central source of truth and execution roadmap:\n\n1. Upon receiving a task, immediately create a lean, focused todo.md with essential sections covering the task lifecycle\n2. Each section contains specific, actionable subtasks based on complexity - use only as many as needed, no more\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Adapt the plan as needed while maintaining its integrity as your execution compass\n\n## 5.2 TODO.MD FILE STRUCTURE AND USAGE\nThe todo.md file is your primary working document and action plan:\n\n1. Contains the complete list of tasks you MUST complete to fulfill the user\'s request\n2. Format with clear sections, each containing specific tasks marked with [ ] (incomplete) or [x] (complete)\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Before every action, consult your todo.md to determine which task to tackle next\n6. The todo.md serves as your instruction set - if a task is in todo.md, you are responsible for completing it\n7. Update the todo.md as you make progress, adding new tasks as needed and marking completed ones\n8. Never delete tasks from todo.md - instead mark them complete with [x] to maintain a record of your work\n9. Once ALL tasks in todo.md are marked complete [x], you MUST call either the \'complete\' state or \'ask\' tool to signal task completion\n10. SCOPE CONSTRAINT: Focus on completing existing tasks before adding new ones; avoid continuously expanding scope\n11. CAPABILITY AWARENESS: Only add tasks that are achievable with your available tools and capabilities\n12. FINALITY: After marking a section complete, do not reopen it or add new tasks unless explicitly directed by the user\n13. STOPPING CONDITION: If you\'ve made 3 consecutive updates to todo.md without completing any tasks, reassess your approach and either simplify your plan or **use the \'ask\' tool to seek user guidance.**\n14. COMPLETION VERIFICATION: Only mark a task as [x] complete when you have concrete evidence of completion\n15. SIMPLICITY: Keep your todo.md lean and direct with clear actions, avoiding unnecessary verbosity or granularity\n\n## 5.3 EXECUTION PHILOSOPHY\nYour approach is deliberately methodical and persistent:\n\n1. Operate in a continuous loop until explicitly stopped\n2. Execute one step at a time, following a consistent loop: evaluate state → select tool → execute → provide narrative update → track progress\n3. Every action is guided by your todo.md, consulting it before selecting any tool\n4. Thoroughly verify each completed step before moving forward\n5. **Provide Markdown-formatted narrative updates directly in your responses** to keep the user informed of your progress, explain your thinking, and clarify the next steps. Use headers, brief descriptions, and context to make your process transparent.\n6. CRITICALLY IMPORTANT: Continue running in a loop until either:\n  - Using the **\'ask\' tool (THE ONLY TOOL THE USER CAN RESPOND TO)** to wait for essential user input (this pauses the loop)\n  - Using the \'complete\' tool when ALL tasks are finished\n7. For casual conversation:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** to properly end the conversation and wait for user input (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n8. For tasks:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** when you need essential user input to proceed (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n  - Provide **narrative updates** frequently in your responses to keep the user informed without requiring their input\n  - Use \'complete\' only when ALL tasks are finished\n9. MANDATORY COMPLETION:\n  - IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after ALL tasks in todo.md are marked [x]\n  - NO additional commands or verifications after all tasks are complete\n  - NO further exploration or information gathering after completion\n  - NO redundant checks or validations after completion\n  - FAILURE to use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after task completion is a critical error\n\n## 5.4 TASK MANAGEMENT CYCLE\n1. STATE EVALUATION: Examine Todo.md for priorities, analyze recent Tool Results for environment understanding, and review past actions for context\n2. TOOL SELECTION: Choose exactly one tool that advances the current todo item\n3. EXECUTION: Wait for tool execution and observe results\n4. **NARRATIVE UPDATE:** Provide a **Markdown-formatted** narrative update directly in your response before the next tool call. Include explanations of what you\'ve done, what you\'re about to do, and why. Use headers, brief paragraphs, and formatting to enhance readability.\n5. PROGRESS TRACKING: Update todo.md with completed items and new tasks\n6. METHODICAL ITERATION: Repeat until section completion\n7. SECTION TRANSITION: Document completion and move to next section\n8. COMPLETION: IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' when ALL tasks are finished\n\n# 6. CONTENT CREATION\n\n## 6.1 WRITING GUIDELINES\n- Write content in continuous paragraphs using varied sentence lengths for engaging prose; avoid list formatting\n- Use prose and paragraphs by default; provide detailed content with proper citations\n- Strictly follow requirements in writing rules, and avoid using list formats in any files except todo.md\n\n## 6.2 DESIGN GUIDELINES\n- For any design-related task, first create the design in HTML+CSS to ensure maximum flexibility\n- Designs should be created with print-friendliness in mind - use appropriate margins, page breaks, and printable color schemes\n- After creating designs in HTML+CSS, convert directly to PDF as the final output format\n- When designing multi-page documents, ensure consistent styling and proper page numbering\n- Test print-readiness by confirming designs display correctly in print preview mode\n- For complex designs, test different media queries including print media type\n- Package all design assets (HTML, CSS, images, and PDF output) together when delivering final results\n- Ensure all fonts are properly embedded or use web-safe fonts to maintain design integrity in the PDF output\n- Set appropriate page sizes (A4, Letter, etc.) in the CSS using @page rules for consistent PDF rendering\n\n## Image Guidelines\n- ALWAYS use the Image Tool for image generation or image editing tasks\n- Write a single self-contained image prompt before calling the Image Tool\n- Clearly describe the main subject and overall composition\n- Explicitly specify the intended visual style and aesthetic\n- Provide exact text content if text is required;            raise ValueError("jitter_range must be between 0 and 1")\n\n\ndef calculate_delay(\n    attempt: int,\n    config: RetryConfig,\n) -> float:\n    """\n    Calculate delay for a given       Delay in seconds\n    """\n    # Calculate exponential delay\n    delay = config.base_delay * (config.exponential_base ** attempt)\n    \n    # Apply maximum cap\n    delay = min(delay, config.max_delay)\n    \n    # Add jitter if enabled\n    if config.jitter:\n        jitter_amount = delay * config.jitter_range\n        delay += random.uniform(-jitter_amount, jitter_amount)\n    \n  \n    Args:\n        error: The exception that occurred\n        config: Retry configuration\n        \n    Returns:\n        True if the error is retryable\n    """\n    # Check if exception type is retryable\n    for retryable_type in config.retryable_exceptions:\n        if isinstance(error, retryable_type):\n            return True\n    \n    # Check for rate limit errors\n    if isinstance(error, RateLimitError):\n        return True\n    \n    # Check for HTTP status codes in certain exceptions\n    if hasattr(error, "status_code"):\n        status_code = getattr(error, "status_code")\n        if status_code in config.retryable_status_codes:\n            return True\n    \n    return False\n\n\ndef with_retry(\n    config: Optional[RetryConfig] = None,\n    *,\n    max_attempts: Optional[int] = None,\n    base_delay: Optional[float] = None,\n    on_retry: Optional[Callable[[int, Exception, float], None]] = None,\n) -> Callable:\n    """\n    Decorator for automatic retry with exponential backoff.\n    \n    Can be used with both sync and async functions.\n    \n    Args:\n        config: RetryConfig instance (uses defaults if not provided)\n        max_attempts: Override max_attempts from config\n        base_delay: Override base_delay from config\n        on_retry: Callback function called on each retry (attempt, error, delay)\n        \n    Returns:\n        Decorated function with retry logic\n        \n    Example:\n        @with_retry(max_attempts=3)\n        async def fetch_data():\n            return await api.get("/data")\n    """\n    # Create or update config\n    if config is None:\n        config = RetryConfig()\n    elif max_attempts is not None or base_delay is not None:\n        # Create a copy with overrides\n exponential_base=config.exponential_base,\n            jitter=config.jitter,\n            jitter_range=config.jitter_range,\n            retryable_exceptions=config.retryable_exceptions,\n            retryable_status_codes=config.retryable_status_codes,\n        )\n    \n    def decorator(func: Callable[P, T]) -> Callable[P, T]:\n        # Check if function is async\n        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(func):\n            @wraps(func)\n            async def async_wrapper(*args: P.args, **kwargs: P.kwargs) -> T:\n                last_error: Optional[Exception] = None\n                \n                for attempt in range(config.max_attempts):\n                    try:\n                        return await func(*args, **kwargs)\n                    except Exception as e:\n                        last_error = e\n                        \n                        # Check if we should retry\n                        if not is_retryable_error(e, config):\n                            raise\n                        \n                        # Check if we\'ve exhausted attempts\n                        if attempt >= config.max_attempts - 1:\n                            raise\n                        \n                        # Calculate delay\n                        delay = calculate_delay(attempt, config)\n                        \n                        # Handle rate limit retry-after header\n                        if isinstance(e, RateLimitError) and e.retry_after:\n                            delay = max(delay, e.retry_after)\n                        \n                        # Call retry callback\n                        if on_retry:\n                            on_retry(attempt + 1, e, delay)\n                        \n                        # Wait before retrying\n                        await asyncio.sleep(delay)\n                \n                # Should not reach here, but raise last error just in case\n                if last_error:\n                    raise last_error\n                raise RuntimeError("Unexpected state in retry logic")\n            \n            return async_wrapper  # type: ignore\n        else:\n            @wraps(func)\n            def sync_wrapper(*args: P.args, **kwargs: P.kwargs) -> T:\n                last_error: Optional[Exception] = None\n                \n                for attempt in raise RuntimeError("Unexpected state in retry logic")\n            \n            return sync_wrapper  # type: ignore\n    \n    return decorator\n\n\nclass Retrier:\n    """\n    Context manager for retry operations.\n    \n    Provides more control over retry behavior with\n    manual iteration support.\n    \n    Example:\n        async with Retrier(config) as retry_ctx:\n            for attempt in retry_ctx:\n                try:\n                    result = await some_operation()\n                    retry_ctx.success()\n                    break\n                except Exception as e:\n                    retry_ctx.set_error(e)\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, config: Optional[RetryConfig] = None):\n        """\n        Initialize retrier.\n        \n        Args:\n            config: Retry configuration\n        """\n        self.config = config or RetryConfig()\n        self.state = RetryState.PENDING\n        self.current_attempt = 0\n        self.last_error: Optional[Exception] = None\n        self._delay_task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None\n    \n    def __iter__(self):\n        """Return self as iterator."""\n        return self\n    \n    def __next__(self) -> int:\n        """Get next attempt number."""\n        if self.state == RetryState.SUCCESS:\n            raise StopIteration\n        \n        if self.current_attempt >= self.config.max_attempts:\n            self.state = RetryState.FAILED\n            raise StopIteration\n        \n        self.current_attempt += 1\n        self.state = RetryState.RETRYING\n -> bool:\n        """Exit async context."""\n        if exc_type is not None:\n            self.last_error = exc_val\n            \n            if is_retryable_error(exc_val, self.config):\n                if self.current_attempt < self.config.max_attempts:\n                    delay = calculate_delay(self.current_attempt - 1, self.config)\n                    await asyncio.sleep(delay)\n operation as successful."""\n        self.state = RetryState.SUCCESS\n    \n    def set_error(self, error: Exception) -> None:\n        """Set the last error."""\n        self.last_error = error\n    \n    def should_retry(self) -> bool:\n        """Check if should retry."""\n        return (\n            self.current_attempt < self.config.max_attempts and\n            self.last_error is not None and\n            is_retryable_error(self.last_error, self.config)\n        )\n    \n    async def wait(self) -> None:\n        """Wait before next attempt."""\n        if self.last_error:\n Escalating to incident."\n)\n```\n\n### Hosts\n\nManage endpoint inventory and isolation.\n\n```python\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.models.hosts import HostState, HostPlatform\n\n# List hosts\nhosts = await client.hosts.list(\n    platform=HostPlatform.WINDOWS,\n    state=HostState.ONLINE,\n    is_isolated=False,\n    limit=100\n)\n\n# Get host details\nhost = await client.hosts.get("host-123")\n\n# Search hosts by hostname\nresults = await client.hosts.search("workstation-")\n\n# Isolate a host\nisolated = await client.hosts.isolate(\n    host_id="host-123",\n    reason="Malware detected - immediate containment required"\n)\n\n# Get host detections\nhost_detections = await client.hosts.get_detections("host-123", limit=20)\n\n# Add tag to host\ntagged = await client.hosts.add_tag("host-123", "investigated")\n```\n\n### Incidents\n\nManage security incident lifecycle.\n\n```python\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.models.incidents import IncidentSeverity, IncidentStatus, IncidentPhase\n\n# Create an incident\nincident = await client.incidents.create(\n    title="Ransomware Detection on Finance Server",\n    description="LockBit ransomware detected on FIN-SRV-01",\n    severity=IncidentSeverity.CRITICAL,\n    hosts=["host-123", "host-456"],\n    detections=["detection-789"],\n    tags=["ransomware", "lockbit", "finance"]\n)\n\n# List incidents\nincidents = await client.incidents.list(\n    severity=IncidentSeverity.CRITICAL,\n    status=IncidentStatus.IN_PROGRESS,\n    time_range="30d"\n)\n\n# Update incident phase\nupdated = await client.incidents.update_phase(\n    incident_id=incident.id,\n    phase=IncidentPhase.CONTAINMENT,\n    notes="Hosts isolated, ransomware binaries removed"\n)\n\n# Add hosts to incident\nupdated = await client.incidents.add_hosts(\n    incident_id=incident.id,\n    host_ids=["host-789"]\n)\n\n# Add timeline entry\ntimeline = await client.incidents.get_timeline(incident.id)\n\n# Close incident\nclosed = await client.incidents.close(\n    incident_id=incident.id,\n    resolution="Ransomware contained and eradicated. Systems restored from backup.",\n    lessons_learned="Consider adding additional email filtering for phishing attachments."\n)\n```\n\n### Threat Intelligence\n\nManage IOCs and threat actor data.\n\n```python\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.models.threat_intel import IOCType, IOCConfidence\n\n# Check an IOC\nresult = await client.threat_intel.check_ioc("malicious.example.com")\n\nif result.is_malicious:\n    print(f"Threat Actor: {result.threat_actor}")\n    print(f"Related IOCs: {len(result.related_iocs)}")\n\n# Bulk check IOCs\nresults = await client.threat_intel.check_iocs_bulk([\n    "192.0.2.1",\n    "malware.hash.example",\n    "https://malicious.url/path"\n])\n\n# Add an IOC\nioc = await client.threat_intel.add_ioc(\n    value="192.0.2.100",\n    ioc_type=IOCType.IP,\n    confidence=IOCConfidence.HIGH,\n    threat_actor="APT29",\n    campaign="CozyBear-2024",\n    malware_family="SUNBURST",\n    tags=["apt29", "supply-chain"],\n    description="C2 server identified in SolarWinds campaign"\n)\n\n# Get threat actor information\nactor = await client.threat_intel.get_threat_actor("APT29")\nprint(f"Aliases: {\', \'.join(actor.aliases)}")\nprint(f"MITRE ID: {actor.mitre_id}")\n\n# Get actor\'s IOCs\nactor_iocs = await client.threat_intel.get_threat_actor_iocs("APT29")\n\n# Export IOCs for SIEM\nsiem_rules = await client.threat_intel.export_for_siEM(\n    siem_type="splunk",\n    ioc_types=[IOCType.IP, IOCType.DOMAIN, IOCType.URL]\n)\n```\n\n## Advanced Configuration\n\n### Custom Retry Configuration\n\n```python\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk import VSentinelClient\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.utils.retry import RetryConfig\n\nretry_config = RetryConfig(\n    max_attempts=5,\n    base_delay=2.0,\n    max_delay=120.0,\n    exponential_base=2.0,\n    jitter=True,\n    retryable_status_codes=[429, 500, 502, 503, 504]\n)\n\nclient = VSentinelClient(\n    api_key="your-api-key",\n    max_retries=5,\n    timeout=60\n)\n```\n\n### Structured Logging\n\n```python\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.utils.logging import configure_logging, LogLevel\n\n# Enable JSON logging\nconfigure_logging(\n Error Handling\n\nThe SDK provides specific exception types for different error scenarios:\n\n```python\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.exceptions import (\n    VSentinelError,\n    AuthenticationError,\n    RateLimitError,\n    ResourceNotFoundError,\n    ValidationError,\n    ConnectionError,\n    TimeoutError,\n)\n\ntry:\n    detection = await client.detections.get("invalid-id")\nexcept ResourceNotFoundError as e:\n    print(f"Resource not found: {e.resource_id}")\nexcept AuthenticationError:\n    print("Invalid API key")\nexcept RateLimitError as e:\n    print(f"Rate limited. Retry after: {e.retry_after} seconds")\nexcept TimeoutError:\n    print("Request timed out")\nexcept VSentinelError as e:\n    print(f"SDK error: {e}")\n```\n\n## Async and Sync Usage\n\nThe SDK is async-first, but you can use it with `asyncio.run()`:\n\n```python\nimport asyncio\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk import VSentinelClient\n\nasync def get_detection(detection_id: str):\n    async with VSentinelClient(api_key="key") as client:\n        return await client.detections.get(detection_id)\n\n# In async context\ndetection = await get_detection("det-123")\n\n# In sync context\ndetection = asyncio.run(get_detection("det-123"))\n```\n\n## Type Hints\n\nAll methods return properly typed Pydantic models:\n\n```python\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.models.detections import Detection, DetectionList\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.models.hosts import Host, HostList\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.models.incidents import Incident, IncidentList\nfrom v_sentinel_sdk.models.threat_intel import IOC, IOCList, IOCCheckResult\n\n# IDE autocomplete and type checking work out of the box\ndetection: Detection = await client.detections.get("det-123")\nhosts: HostList = await client.hosts.list()\n```\n\n## Development\n\n### Setup Development Environment\n\n```bash\n# Clone the repository\ngit clone https://github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdks.git\ncd v-sentinel-sdks/python\n\n# Create virtual environment\npython -m venv .venv\nsource .venv/bin/activate  # or .venv\\Scripts\\activate on Windows\n\n# Install development dependencies\npip install -e ".[dev]"\n\n# Run tests\npytest\n\n# Run type checking\nmypy v_sentinel_sdk\n\n# Format code\nblack v_sentinel_sdk\nruff check v_sentinel_sdk\n```\n\n### Running Tests\n\n```bash\n# Run all tests\npytest\n\n# Run with coverage\npytest --cov=v_sentinel_sdk --cov-report=html\n\n# Run specific test file\npytest tests/test_detections.py\n\n# Run with verbose output\npytest -v\n```\n\n## License\n\nThis project is licensed under the MIT License - Limit:    10,\n//\t})\npackage vsentinel\n\nimport (\n\t"context"\n\t"fmt"\n\t"net/http"\n\t"net/url"\n\t"time"\n\n\t"github.com/go-resty/resty/v2"\n)\n\nconst (\n\t// DefaultBaseURL is the default NewClient(apiKey string, opts ...ClientOption) (*Client, error) {\n\tif apiKey == "" {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf("API key is required")\n\t}\n\n\t// Parse default base URL\n\tbaseURL, err := ||\n\t\t\tr.StatusCode() == http.StatusServiceUnavailable ||\n\t\t\tr.StatusCode() == http.StatusGatewayTimeout\n\t})\n\n\tclient := &Client{\n\t\thttp:    httpClient,\n\t\tbaseURL: baseURL,\n\t\tapiKey:  apiKey,\n\t}\n\n\t// Apply options\n\tfor _, opt := range opts {\n\t\tif err := opt(client); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Set map[string]string, result interface{}) error {\n\treq := c.newRequest(ctx).SetResult(result)\n\n\tif len(params) > 0 {\n\t\treq.SetQueryParams(params)\n\t}\n\n\tresp, err := req.Get(c.baseURL.String() {\n\t\tparams["limit"] = "50"\n\t}\n\n\terr := s.client.get(ctx, "/threat-intel/campaigns", params, &result)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn &result, nil\n}\n\n// GetCampaign "/threat-intel/campaigns/"+campaignID, nil, &result)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn &result, nil\n}\n\n// GetCampaignIOCs retrieves IOCs associated with a campaign.\nfunc (s string\n\tMalwareFamily  string\n\tTags           []string\n\tFormat         string\n\tIncludeExpired bool\n}\n\n// Export exports IOCs in the specified format.\nfunc (s *ThreatIntelService) Export(ctx context.Context, opts *ExportOptions) (string, error) {\n\tparams := map[string]string{\n\t\t"format": opts.Format,\n\t}\n\n\tif opts.Type != "" {\n\t\tparams["type"] = string(opts.Type)\n\t}\n\tif opts.ThreatActor != "" {\n\t\tparams["threat_actor"] = opts.ThreatActor\n\t}\n\tif opts.MalwareFamily != "" {\n\t\tparams["malware_family"] = opts.MalwareFamily\n\t}\n\tif len(opts.Tags) > 0 {\n\t\tparams["tags"] = joinStrings(opts.Tags, ",")\n\t}\n\tif opts.IncludeExpired {\n\t\tparams["include_expired"] = "true"\n\t}\n\n\tvar result string\n\n\terr := Provides a comprehensive client for interacting with V-Sentinel APIs, including detections, hosts, incidents, and threat intelligence operations.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Simple and intuitive API** - Clean Go idioms with proper error handling\n- **Context support** - All operations support context for cancellation and timeouts\n- **Automatic retries** - Built-in retry logic with exponential backoff\n- **Type-safe** - Strong typing with Go structs for all API responses\n- **Comprehensive coverage** - Full API coverage for all V-Sentinel operations\n- **Zero dependencies** - Minimal external dependencies (just go-resty)\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\ngo get github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdk-go\n```\n\n## Quick Start\n\n```go\npackage main\n\nimport (\n    "context"\n    "fmt"\n    "log"\n\n    vsentinel "github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdk-go"\n)\n\nfunc main() {\n    // Create client\n    client, err := vsentinel.NewClient("your-api-key")\n    if err != nil {\n        log.Fatal(err)\n    }\n\n    ctx := context.Background()\n\n    // List recent critical detections\n    detections, err := client.Detections.List(ctx, &vsentinel.DetectionListOptions{\n        Severity: vsentinel.SeverityCritical,\n        TimeRange: "24h",\n        Limit:    10,\n    })\n    if err != nil {\n        log.Fatal(err)\n    }\n\n    for _, det := range detections.Items {\n        fmt.Printf("[%s] %s\\n", det.Severity, det.Title)\n        fmt.Printf("  Host: %s\\n", det.Host.Hostname)\n        fmt.Printf("  MITRE Techniques: %v\\n", det.Techniques)\n    }\n\n    // Check an IOC against threat intelligence\n    result, err := client.ThreatIntel.CheckIOC(ctx, "192.0.2.1", vsentinel.IOCTypeIP)\n    if err != nil {\n        log.Fatal(err)\n    }\n\n    if result.IsMalicious {\n        fmt.Printf("Malicious IOC detected!\\n")\n        fmt.Printf("  Threat Actor: %s\\n", result.ThreatActor)\n        fmt.Printf("  Confidence: %s\\n", result.Confidence)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Authentication\n\n### API Key\n\n```go\nclient, err := vsentinel.NewClient("your-api-key")\n```\n\n### Environment Variable\n\n```go\nimport "os"\n\nclient, err := vsentinel.NewClient(os.Getenv("V_SENTINEL_API_KEY"))\n```\n\n### Custom Configuration\n\n```go\nclient, err := vsentinel.NewClient(\n    "your-api-key",\n    vsentinel.WithBaseURL("https://api.custom.com/v1"),\n    vsentinel.WithTimeout(60 * time.Second),\n    vsentinel.WithMaxRetries(5),\n    vsentinel.WithProxy("http://proxy.company.com:8080"),\n    vsentinel.WithDebug(true),\n)\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Detections\n\nManage security detections and alerts.\n\n```go\n// List detections with filters\ndetections, err := client.Detections.List(ctx, &vsentinel.DetectionListOptions{\n    Severity:  vsentinel.SeverityHigh,\n    Status:    vsentinel.DetectionStatusNew,\n    TimeRange: "7d",\n    HostID:    "host-123",\n    Limit:     50,\n})\n\n// Get a specific detection\ndetection, err := client.Detections.Get(ctx, "detection-456")\n\n// Update detection status\nupdated, err := client.Detections.UpdateStatus(ctx, "detection-456", &vsentinel.UpdateStatusOptions{\n    Status: vsentinel.DetectionStatusInProgress,\n    Notes:  "Investigating potential false positive",\n})\n\n// Assign detection to analyst\nassigned, err := client.Detections.Assign(ctx, "detection-456", "analyst@company.com")\n\n// Add note to detection\nnote, err := client.Detections.AddNote(ctx, "detection-456", "Confirmed as true positive")\n```\n\n### Hosts\n\nManage endpoint inventory and isolation.\n\n```go\n// List hosts\nhosts, err := client.Hosts.List(ctx, &vsentinel.HostListOptions{\n    Platform: hostname\nresults, err := client.Hosts.Search(ctx, "workstation-", 50)\n\n// Isolate a host\nisolated, err := client.Hosts.Isolate(ctx, "host-123", "Malware detected - immediate containment required")\n\n// Get host detections\nhostDetections, err := client.Hosts.GetDetections(ctx, "host-123", 20)\n\n// Add tag to host\ntagged, err := client.Hosts.AddTag(ctx, "host-123", "investigated")\n```\n\n### Incidents\n\nManage security incident lifecycle.\n\n```go\n// Create an incident\nincident, err := client.Incidents.Create(ctx, &vsentinel.IncidentCreateOptions{\n    Title:       "Ransomware Detection on Finance Server",\n    Description: "LockBit ransomware detected on FIN-SRV-01",\n    Severity:    vsentinel.IncidentSeverityCritical,\n    Hosts: "malware.hash.example",\n    "https://malicious.url/path",\n}, vsentinel.IOCTypeIP)\n\n// Add an IOC\nioc, err := client.ThreatIntel.AddIOC(ctx, &vsentinel.AddIOCOptions{\n    Value:         "192.0.2.100",\n    Type:          vsentinel.IOCTypeIP,\n    Confidence:    vsentinel.ConfidenceHigh,\n    ThreatActor:   "APT29",\n    Campaign:      "CozyBear-2024",\n    MalwareFamily: "github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdk-go"\n)\n\ndetection, err := client.Detections.Get(ctx, "invalid-id")\nif err != nil {\n    var notFound *vsentinel.ResourceNotFoundError\n    var authError *vsentinel.AuthenticationError\n    var rateLimit *vsentinel.RateLimitError\n    \n    switch {\n    case errors.As(err, &notFound):\n        fmt.Printf("Resource not found: %s\\n", notFound.ResourceID)\n    case errors.As(err, &authError):\n        fmt.Println("Invalid API key")\n    case errors.As(err, &rateLimit):\n        fmt.Printf("Rate limited. Retry after: %s\\n", rateLimit.RetryAfter)\n    default:\n        fmt.Printf("Error: %v\\n", err)\n    }\n}\n\n// Helper functions\nif vsentinel.IsNotFoundError(err) {\n    // Handle not found\n}\n```\n\n## Context and Timeouts\n\nAll operations support context for cancellation and timeouts:\n\n```go\n// With timeout\nctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 30*time.Second)\ndefer cancel()\n\ndetections, err := client.Detections.List(ctx, nil)\n\n// With cancellation\nctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\ngo func() {\n    time.Sleep(5 * time.Second)\n    cancel() // Cancel after 5 seconds\n}()\n\ndetections, err := client.Detections.List(ctx, nil)\nif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n    // Handle cancellation\n}\n```\n\n## Retries\n\nThe SDK automatically retries on transient errors:\n\n```go\nclient, err := vsentinel.NewClient(\n    "your-api-key",\n    vsentinel.WithMaxRetries(5),\n)\n```\n\nDefault retry behavior:\n- Retries on: 429, 500, 502, 503, 504 status codes\n- Exponential backoff: 1s → 2s → 4s → ... (max 30s)\n- Respects `Retry-After` header for 429 responses\n\n## Proxy Configuration\n\n```go\n// HTTP proxy\nclient, err := vsentinel.NewClient(\n    "your-api-key",\n    vsentinel.WithProxy("http://proxy.company.com:8080"),\n)\n\n// SOCKS5 proxy\nclient, err := vsentinel.NewClient(\n    "your-api-key",\n    vsentinel.WithProxy("socks5://proxy.company.com:1080"),\n)\n```\n\n## Development\n\n### Requirements\n\n- Go 1.21 or later\n\n### Running Tests\n\n```bash\ngo test ./...\n```\n\n### Linting\n\n```bash\ngo vet ./...\ngolangci-lint run\n```\n\n## License\n\nThis project is licensed under the MIT License - see the [LICENSE](LICENSE) file for details.\n\n## Support\n\n- **Documentation**: [https://docs.vantis.ai/sdks/go](https://docs.vantis.ai/sdks/go)\n- **API Reference**: [https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdk-go](https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdk-go)\n- **GitHub Issues**: [https://github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdks/issues](https://github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdks/issues)\n- **Security Issues**: security@vantis.ai\n\n## Contributing\n\nWe welcome contributions! different API error scenarios.\n */\n\n/** Base error class for all V-Sentinel SDK errors */\nexport class VSentinelError extends Error {\n  constructor(message: string) {\n    super(message);\n    this.name = \'VSentinelError\';\n    Object.setPrototypeOf(this, VSentinelError.prototype);\n  }\n}\n\n/** API error with status code and response details */\nexport class APIError extends VSentinelError {\n  readonly statusCode: number;\n  readonly response?: unknown;\n\n  constructor(statusCode: number, message: string, response?: unknown) {\n    super(message);\n    this.name = \'APIError\';\n    this.statusCode = statusCode;\n    this.response = response;\n    Object.setPrototypeOf(this, APIError.prototype);\n  }\n}\n\n/** Authentication failure (401 or 403) */\nexport class AuthenticationError extends VSentinelError {\n  constructor(message: string = \'Authentication failed\') {\n    super(message);\n    this.name = \'AuthenticationError\';\n    Object.setPrototypeOf(this, AuthenticationError.prototype);\n  }\n}\n\n/** Resource not found (404) */\nexport class ResourceNotFoundError extends VSentinelError {\n  readonly resourceType?: string;\n  readonly resourceId?: string;\n\n  constructor(\n    message: string,\n    resourceType?: string,\n    resourceId?: string\n  ) {\n    super(message);\n    this.name = \'ResourceNotFoundError\';\n    this.resourceType = resourceType;\n    this.resourceId = resourceId;\n    Object.setPrototypeOf(this, ResourceNotFoundError.prototype);\n  }\n}\n\n/** Validation error (400) */\nexport class ThreatIntelService;\n\n  constructor(options: ClientOptions) {\n    if (!options.apiKey) {\n      throw new Error(\'API key is required\');\n    }\n\n    this.baseURL = options.baseURL ?? DEFAULT_MAX_RETRIES;\n\n    // Create axios instance\n    this.httpClient = axios.create({\n      baseURL: this.baseURL,\n      timeout,\n      headers: {\n        \'Accept\': \'application/json\',\n        \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\',\n        \'User-Agent\': `v-sentinel-sdk-ts/${VERSION}`,\n        \'Authorization\': `Bearer ${options.apiKey}`,\n        ...options.headers,\n      },\n      proxy: options.proxy ? \'Authentication failed\');\n    }\n\n    if (status === 404) {\n      throw new ResourceNotFoundError(\n        data?.message ?? \'Resource not found\'\n      );\n    }\n\n    if (status === 429) {\n      const retryAfter = response?.headers[\'retry-after\'];\n      throw new RateLimitError(\n        data?.message ?? \'Rate limit exceeded\',\n        retryAfter ? parseInt(retryAfter) : undefined\n      );\n    }\n\n    if (status === 400) {\n      throw new ValidationError(\n        data?.message ?? \'Validation failed\',\n        data?.details\n      );\n    }\n\n    if (status && status >= 500) {\n      throw new APIError(\n        status,\n        data?.message ?? \'Internal server error\',\n        data\n      );\n    }\n\n    if (error.code === \'ECONNABORTED\' || error.code === \'ETIMEDOUT\') {\n      throw new TimeoutError(\'Request timed out\');\n    }\n\n    if (error.code === \'ECONNREFUSED\' || error.code === \'ENOTFOUND\') {\n      throw new ConnectionError(`Connection failed: ${error.message}`);\n    }\n\n    throw new APIError(\n      status ?? 0,\n      data?.message ?? error.message,\n      data\n    );\n  }\n\n  if (error instanceof Error) {\n    throw error;\n  }\n\n  throw new Error(\'Unknown error occurred\');\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

DetectionStatus.InProgress,\n  notes: \'Investigating potential false positive\',\n});\n\n// Assign detection to analyst\nconst assigned = await client.detections.assign(\n  \'detection-456\',\n  \'analyst@company.com\'\n);\n\n// Add note to detection\nconst note = await client.detections.addNote(\n  \'detection-456\',\n  \'Confirmed as true positive\'\n);\n```\n\n### Hosts\n\nManage endpoint inventory and isolation.\n\n```typescript\nimport { HostPlatform, HostState } from \'@vantis/v-sentinel-sdk\';\n\n// List hosts\nconst hosts = await client.hosts.list({\n  platform: HostPlatform.Windows,\n  state: HostState.Online,\n  isIsolated: false,\n  limit: 100,\n});\n\n// Get host details\nconst host = await client.hosts.get(\'host-123\');\n\n// Search hosts by hostname\nconst results = await client.hosts.search(\'workstation-\', 50);\n\n// Isolate a host\nconst isolated = await client.hosts.isolate(\n  \'host-123\',\n  \'Malware detected - immediate containment required\'\n);\n\n// Get host detections\nconst hostDetections = await client.hosts.getDetections(\'host-123\', 20);\n\n// Add tag to host\nconst tagged = await client.hosts.addTag(\'host-123\', \'investigated\');\n```\n\n### Incidents\n\nManage security incident lifecycle.\n\n```typescript\nimport {\n  IncidentSeverity,\n  IncidentStatus,\n  IncidentPhase\n} from \'@vantis/v-sentinel-sdk\';\n\n// Create an incident\nconst incident = await client.incidents.create({\n  title: \'Ransomware Detection on Finance Server\',\n  description: \'LockBit ransomware detected on FIN-SRV-01\',\n  severity: IncidentSeverity.Critical,\n  hosts: [\'host-123\', \'host-456\'],\n  detections: [\'detection-789\'],\n  tags: [\'ransomware\', \'lockbit\', \'finance\'],\n});\n\n// List incidents\nconst incidents = await client.incidents.list({\n  severity: IncidentSeverity.Critical,\n  status: IncidentStatus.InProgress,\n  timeRange: \'30d\',\n});\n\n// Update incident phase\nconst updated = await client.incidents.updatePhase(incident.id, {\n  phase: IncidentPhase.Containment,\n  notes: \'Hosts isolated, ransomware binaries removed\',\n});\n\n// Add hosts to incident\nconst withHosts = await client.incidents.addHosts(incident.id, [\'host-789\']);\n\n// Close incident\nconst closed = await client.incidents.close(incident.id, {\n  resolution: \'Ransomware contained and eradicated. Systems restored from backup.\',\n  lessonsLearned: \'Consider adding additional email filtering for phishing attachments.\',\n});\n```\n\n### Threat Intelligence\n\nManage IOCs and threat actor data.\n\n```typescript\nimport { IOCType, IOCConfidence } from \'@vantis/v-sentinel-sdk\';\n\n// Check an IOC\nconst result = await client.threatIntel.checkIOC(\'malicious.example.com\');\n\nif (result.isMalicious) {\n  console.log(`Threat Actor: ${result.threatActor}`);\n  console.log(`Related IOCs: ${result.relatedIOCs?.length}`);\n}\n\n// Bulk check IOCs\nconst results = await client.threatIntel.checkIOCsBulk([\n  \'192.0.2.1\',\n  \'malware.hash.example\',\n  \'https://malicious.url/path\',\n]);\n\n// Add an IOC\nconst ioc = await client.threatIntel.addIOC({\n  value: \'192.0.2.100\',\n  type: IOCType.IP,\n  confidence: IOCConfidence.High,\n  threatActor: \'APT29\',\n  campaign: \'CozyBear-2024\',\n  malwareFamily: \'SUNBURST\',\n  tags: [\'apt29\', \'supply-chain\'],\n  description: \'C2 server identified in SolarWinds campaign\',\n});\n\n// Get threat actor information\nconst actor = await client.threatIntel.getThreatActor(\'APT29\');\nconsole.log(`Aliases: ${actor.aliases?.join(\', \')}`);\nconsole.log(`MITRE ID: ${actor.mitreId}`);\n\n// Get actor\'s IOCs\nconst actorIOCs = await client.threatIntel.getThreatActorIOCs(\'APT29\');\n\n// Export IOCs for SIEM\nconst siemRules = await client.threatIntel.exportForSIEM(\n  \'splunk\',\n  [IOCType.IP, IOCType.Domain, IOCType.URL]\n);\n```\n\n## Error Handling\n\nThe SDK provides specific error types for different scenarios:\n\n```typescript\nimport {\n  VSentinelError,\n  AuthenticationError,\n  RateLimitError,\n  ResourceNotFoundError,\n  ValidationError,\n  isRateLimitError,\n} from \'@vantis/v-sentinel-sdk\';\n\ntry {\n  const detection = await client.detections.get(\'invalid-id\');\n} catch (error) {\n  if (error instanceof ResourceNotFoundError) {\n    console.log(`Resource not found: ${error.resourceId}`);\n  } else if (error instanceof AuthenticationError) {\n    console.log(\'Invalid API key\');\n  } else if (isRateLimitError(error)) {\n    console.log(`Rate limited. Retry after: ${error.retryAfter} seconds`);\n  } else if (error instanceof ValidationError) {\n    console.log(`Validation failed: ${error.message}`);\n    console.log(\'Details:\', error.details);\n  } else {\n    console.log(\'Error:\', error);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Configuration Options\n\n```typescript\ninterface ClientOptions {\n  /** API key for authentication (required) */\n  apiKey: string;\n\n  /** Base URL for API requests */\n  baseURL?: string;  // default: \'https://api.vantis.ai/v1\'\n\n  /** Request timeout in milliseconds */\n  timeout?: number;  // default: 30000\n\n  /** Maximum number of retries */\n  maxRetries?: number;  // default: 3\n\n  /** Proxy URL */\n  proxy?: string;\n\n  /** Enable debug logging */\n  debug?: boolean;\n\n  /** Custom HTTP headers */\n  headers?: Record<string, string>;\n}\n```\n\n## Retries\n\nThe SDK automatically retries on transient errors:\n\n- Retries on: 429, 500, 502, 503, 504 status codes\n- Exponential backoff: 1s → 2s → 4s → ... (max 30s)\n- Respects `Retry-After` header for 429 responses\n\n## Development\n\n### Requirements\n\n- Node.js 18.0.0 or later\n- npm, yarn, or pnpm\n\n### Build\n\n```bash\nnpm run build\n```\n\n### Test\n\n```bash\nnpm test\n\n# With coverage\nnpm run test:coverage\n```\n\n### Lint\n\n```bash\nnpm run lint\nnpm run lint:fix\n```\n\n## License\n\nThis project is licensed under the MIT License - see the [LICENSE](LICENSE) file for details.\n\n## Support\n\n- **Documentation**: [https://docs.vantis.ai/sdks/typescript](https://docs.vantis.ai/sdks/typescript)\n- **API Reference**: [https://api.vantis.ai/docs](https://api.vantis.ai/docs)\n- **GitHub Issues**: [https://github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdks/issues](https://github.com/vantis-ai/v-sentinel-sdks/issues)\n- **Security Issues**: security@vantis.ai\n\n## Contributing\n\nWe welcome contributions!
